 action 3.0 regexp "RUNNING" "$_cli_result" line
 action 4.0 if $_regexp_result eq "0"
 action 4.5  syslog msg "EEM: Guestshell not running"
 action 5.0  cli command "guestshell enable"
 action 6.0 end
!
